Must: return 3, 0x8(%rsp) = 3
p1 <= 14
func_rec(int p1, int p2, int p3) {
  val = (p3 - p2) /2 + p2; //r1 = 7
  if (p1 < val) {
    val1 = func_rec(p1, p2, val - 1);
    return 2*val1;
  }
  if (p1 > val) {
    val1 = func_rec(p1, val + 1, p3);
    return 2*val1 + 1
  }
  return 0; only if p1 == val
}
0 -> 1 -> 3 -> done
p1 == val, p1 > val, p1 > val
p1 = 13 (12,14)(8,14)(0,14)
p1 = 13 ->
f1: 13, 0, 14) -> val = 7, func_rec(13, 8, 14) return 3
f2: 13, 8, 14) -> val = 11, func_rec(13, 12, 14) return 1
f3: 13, 12, 14) -> val = 13, 0
